 Under this scheme, people who have not paid the entire tax before have been given the opportunity to declare undisclosed income and assets
 isaki shuruyaat 1 june 2016 ko hui or yah 30 sitambar 2016 tak khulaa he
 Notification of rules related to the scheme was issued on 19 May 2016
 kishton main hoga rakam kaa bhugtanyojna ke bhugtan kishton main kiya ja saktaa he

 nahin hoga yojana ke samay main koi vistaaryojna ke niyamon ke tahat pramukh muddon ko spasht karte hue sawaalon ko saamne laayaa gaya he
 The Ministry has reiterated that the scheme is going to close on 30 September 2016
 is yojana ke vistaar kaa koi maamla hi nahin he
 Some of the major questions asked by those who declare income are- • The information of valid declaration will be completely confidential
 ise na hi kisi bheekanoon pravartan agencyke saath saajha kiya jayega or na hi iskar vibhaag kii ore se jaancha jayega
 • The income declared under the scheme will be determined as of 1 June 2016 based on the cost of acquisition or fair market value (whichever is higher in both)
 haalanki, samyojit adhigrahan ke stamp shulk mulya ke aadhaar par darj achal sampatti ke moolyankan ke liye laagat mudrasphiti suchakank ke rup main bhi ek vikalp maujuud he
 • Credit of TDS made without claim will be allowed on declared income
 • benami sampatti ko benamidaar se ghoshit karne vaale vyakti ke naam hastantaran main na hi koicapital taxdena hoga or na hi tids lagegaa
 • Assets declared under it will neither be recorded as fake liabilities in the audited balance sheet nor can the amount associated with the acquisition of the asset be disclosed under such scheme

 aapako bataa den ki ye sara maamla baaluu ko lekar hua he

 jiske praavdhaanon ko lekar jabardast virodh ho rahaa he

 " Ghee and pure butter are two foods that are very important for your diet in winter
 ye desi rasoi main hone vaale aise superfood hai jo sardiyon main sabase zyada istemaal kiye jate hai
 The biggest benefits of using them are their benefits
 ghi ke bare main kaha jaataa he ki sardiyon main hamaare sharir ko ye andar se garm rakhata he, jisase kii sardiyon kaa vipareet prabhaav aapke sharir par nahin padataa he
 The nature of ghee in the Aryurveda is called a heat-producing food
 thand ke mausam main subjiyon or soup main desi ghi ke istemaal kii salaah di jaati he

 Unsaturated fat or healthy fat in ghee helps in correcting the good cholesterol level in the blood
it also reduces weight due to the high healdi fat kii ghi main adhikta hone kii vazah se yah vazan ko bhi kam karata he
 Ghee also has an advantage that often does not go unnoticed
 ghi kaa ye khaas gun ise sardiyon main superfood banaata he
